My family was spending the weekend, and I thought the price-performance ratio for two rooms at more than 1,000 yuan was really good.
However, I don‚Äôt require the hotel‚Äôs service to be very good, it should be more or less consistent with common sense, right? On the first day of check-in, I drove to the hotel entrance, and the concierge didn't even help me with my luggage. I took two pieces of luggage with my children and elders to the lobby to check in, and the concierge took a look and left. The girl at the front desk didn't even have polite words to speak, and she couldn't even say hello. There was a guy next to her who was answering questions for her and introducing breakfast and so on.
Because breakfast was not included in the room rate, I prepaid for breakfast for two days separately. The next day because our daughter got up late, we didn't go downstairs to eat. When I checked out, I asked if the breakfast fee for the next day could be refunded. The front desk said no. We need to inform them one day in advance, otherwise they will not be refunded. They told the front desk when we checked in. I must have said that.
Excuse me???
First of all, she 100% didn‚Äôt tell me when she checked in, and she swiped the wrong card when charging. She swiped my card an extra 200 yuan and said she would deduct two days of breakfast from me, but the first swipe was only for the first day of the reservation. I haven't told her yet that I want to extend my stay.
Secondly, in what era are we now, do we still have this kind of overlord clause? I paid and didn‚Äôt eat, so why don‚Äôt I get a refund? It‚Äôs not that I went to a restaurant to order food and you refused to refund it if I ordered it, or it‚Äôs not that I didn‚Äôt eat the meal myself as the room rate included meals. If it was the case of these two situations, I would never unreasonably ask for a refund.
Although I refunded the money in the end, it was because the front desk made the wrong payment. Otherwise, judging from the appearance of the front desk, I would have been fighting for a long time without refunding. I told her that I was a black diamond and had stayed in so many hotels. I had never had to tell the hotel a day in advance if I didn‚Äôt want to eat. She smiled contemptuously and I still remember her expression to this day.
I have stayed in many five-star hotels in Beijing. I have been in Beijing for more than ten years, and I understand the culture of Beijing. No matter how good the hardware is, the service may not be very warm and thoughtful, but this experience at Quintiles is really amazing. It gave me some knowledge.
